Rating Points|
收视率（Rating Points）|
~
The rating points of the media in which the product is being advertised. It tells you how many people are watching the media. Thus, the higher the rating points, the greater the effect of the advertising.^|
收视率意味着产品在媒体内被广告后看到的机会。它会告诉你有多少人在观看该节目。^^因此，该数值越高，广告效果越好。|

Expansion Strategies|
扩张策略|
~
Management Policies|
管理政策|
~
This determines whether the CEO may build factories, farms and natural resource firms to supply raw materials and semi products to existing factories that need them. The higher the slider's value, the higher the tendency to set up firms for backward integration.|
这决定了CEO是否可以建立工厂，农场和自然资源采集企业来供应原材料和半成品去
支持他们的上游工厂。滑块的值越高，代表越倾向扩张下游产业链。|
~
CEO Policy on Issuing New Shares|
首席执行官发行新股政策|
~
If this is turned off, the CEO will never issue new shares for expanding the business. But if the company is out of cash, the CEO will have to issue new shares to raise funds for the company's survival regardless of this setting.|
但是，如果公司资金链断裂，CEO为了公司的生存将被迫发行新股筹集资金|

Double-click on a product class on the list to change its ink color, which can be:

RED - it means that the CEO should NOT produce any products in the product class.

BLACK - it means that the CEO may produce products in the product class.|
双击列表上的一个产品类别，以改变它的颜色，这可以：
红色-这意味着，首席执行官不应该生产任何产品在产品类别。
黑色-这意味着首席执行官可能产生的产品类产品。|
